SPECIAL NOTICE

AS Friday, 25th December, 2009, will be a Christmas Holiday, the Issue of the Kenya Gazette that should have been published on that day will now be published on Thursday, 24th December, 2009.

A. G. RUKARIA, Government Printer.

THE KENYA GAZETTE

Published by Authority of the Republic of Kenya

(Registered as a Newspaper at the G.P.O.)

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13507</span>
THE VALUATION FOR RATING ACT ( Cap. 266)

THE COUNTY COUNCIL OF KWALE DECLARATION

IN  EXERCISE  of  the  powers  conferred  by  section  6  of  the Valuation for Rating Act, the Deputy Prime Minister and Minister for Local Government  declare that 'valuer in preparing any Draft Valuation  Roll  or  Draft  Supplementary  Valuation  Roll,  need  neither value nor include in the roll the value of the land or the assessment for improvement rate, as required by paragraphs (c) and (e) respectively of this section'.

Dated the 1st December, 2009.

MUSALIA MUDAVADI, Deputy Prime Minister and Minister for Local Government.

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13508</span>
THE RATING ACT

( Cap. 267)

THE COUNTY COUNCIL OF KWALE

SITE VALUE RATE

IN EXERCISE of the powers conferred by section 4 (1) (b) of the Rating  Act,  the  Deputy  Prime  Minister  and  Minister  for  Local Government approves adoption by County Council of Kwale of a 'site value' for purposes of levying rates.

Dated the 1st December, 2009.

MUSALIA MUDAVADI, Deputy Prime Minister and Minister for Local Government.

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13518</span>
THE MINING ACT

( Cap . 306)

APPLICATION FOR A SPECIAL LICENCE

NOTICE  is  given  that  an  application  under  Section  17  of  the Mining Act has been made by Messrs Abba Mining Company Ltd of P.O. Box 1112, Kisumu, Kenya for a special licence to prospect for all minerals  over  an  area  described  in  the  schedule  hereto  and  the  said application has been accepted for consideration.

By virtue of the above mentioned section of the Mining Act, the said area of land is therefore re-opened to prospecting and mining and by virtue of section 7(1) (d) of the same Act, the said area of land is excluded  from  prospecting  and  or  mining  except  as  regards  any prospecting and mining rights granted in respect of the area or any part thereof before the date of this notice which are subsisting or any right of renewal thereof.

Any objection to the grant of the special licence may be made in writing  and  addressed  to  the  Commissioner  of  Mines  and  Geology, P.O. Box 30009 - 00100, G.P.O, Nairobi, Kenya to reach him within thirty (30) days from the date of publication of this notice.

SCHEDULE

An area  of  approximately  112  km 2 situated  in  Rongo  District  of Nyanza Province, delineated on Kisumu Topo sheet Ref No. SA-36-4 of scale 1:250,000 and more particularly described as follows-

Commencing at point 'A' grid reference XQ 7333, thence on a grid bearing of 90 0 for a distance of approximately 5 km to point 'B' grid reference XQ 7833, thence on a grid bearing of 180 0 for a distance of approximately 2 km to point 'C' grid reference XQ 7831, thence on a grid bearing of 90 0 for a distance of approximately 2 km to point 'D' grid reference XQ 8031, thence on a grid bearing of 180 0 for a distance of approximately 3 km to point 'E' grid reference XQ 8028; thence on a grid bearing of 90 0 for a distance of approximately 2 km to point 'F' grid reference XQ 8228, thence on a grid bearing of 180 0 for a distance of approximately 9 km to point 'G' grid reference XQ 8219, thence on a grid bearing of 270 0 for  a  distance  of  approximately 9 km to point 'H' grid reference XQ 7319, thence on a grid bearing of 360 0 for  a distance of approximately 14 km to the point of commencement.

B. K. ROP,

Commissioner of Mines and Geology.

THE REGISTRATION OF TITLES ACT ( Cap. 281, section 71)

ISSUE OF A PROVISIONAL CERTIFICATE

WHEREAS The Minister of Public Building and Works of the United Kingdom,  is  the  registered  proprietor  lessee  of  that  piece  of  land known as L.R. No. 209/6267, situate in the city of Nairobi, by virtue of a grant registered as I.R. 19424/1, and whereas sufficient evidence has been adduced to show that the said certificate of title issued thereof has been lost, notice is given that after the expiration of ninety (90) days from  the  date  hereof,  I  shall  issue  a  provisional  certificate  of  title provided that no objection has been received within that period.

Dated the 18th December, 2009.

C. N. KITUYI, Registrar of Titles, Nairobi.

THE REGISTRATION OF TITLES ACT ( Cap. 281)

REGISTRATION OF INSTRUMENT

WHEREAS  Nakuru  Mutukanio  Farmers  Companies  Limited,  a limited liability company incorporated in Kenya having its registered office,  of  P.O.  Box  47089,  Nairobi  in  the  Republic  of  Kenya,  is registered proprietor lessee of that piece of land containing 2000 acres or  thereabout,  known  as  L.R.  No.  10244(Original  No.  2956/2/1/1), situate  in  the  south  of  Nakuru  Municipality  in  Nakuru,  held  under grant registered as I.R. 20578/1, and whereas Kenya Commercial Bank Limited, a limited liability company incorporated in Kenya having its registered office at Nairobi, has executed an instrument of discharge of charge  in  favour  of  the  said  Nakuru  Mutukanio  Farmers  Companies Limited, and whereas affidavits have been filled in terms of section 65 (1) ( h ) of the said Act, declaring that the said grant registered as No. I.R 20578/1 is not available for registration, notice is given that after the expiration of fourteen (14) days from the date hereof provided that no  valid  objection  has  been  received  within  that  period,  I  intend  to dispense  with  the  production  of  the  said  grant  and  proceed  with  the registration of the said instrument of discharge of charge.

Dated the 18th December, 2009.

C. N. KITUYI, Registrar of Titles, Nairobi.

PROBATE AND ADMINISTRATION

TAKE NOTICE that after thirty (30) days from the date of this Gazette, and unless cause be shown to the contrary, I intend to apply to the High Court  at  Kisumu    for  representation  of  the  estates  of  the  persons  named  in  the  second  column  of  the  schedule  hereto,  who  died  on  the  dates respectively set forth against their names.

And further take notice that all persons having any claims against or interests in the estates of the said deceased persons are required to prove such claims or interests before me within two (2) months from the date of this Gazette, after which date the claims and interests are proved will be paid and satisfied and the several estates distributed according to law.

DRIVE, LAVINGTON, NAIROBI I NVITATION OF PUBLIC COMMENTS PURSUANT to regulation 21 of Environmental (Impact Assessment and Audit) Regulations, the National Environment Management Authority (NEMA) has received an Environmental Impact Assessment Study Report for the implementation of the Proposed Stream Canalization and Realignment on L.R. NO. 3734/549/45 Along Chalbi Drive, Lavington, Nairobi. The proponent intends to divert the Katina river channel (which | emissions Noise pollution |  |  Maintain plant equipment (if
flows in the middle of the plot), through an appropriately designed box channel running parallel to the northern boundary of the plot without disturbing the existing NCC sewer line. The project anticipates the following impacts and mitigation measures:- Possible Impacts Mitigation Measures Protection of the stream canal    The proper | CCN and Nairobi Water and Sewerage company should ensure all sewer waste in the slums is connected to the improved sewer system Ensure all the recharge areas on the lower part of the plot are not blocked anti-pollution measures | Oil pollution | present/used)  Construction activities to be restricted to daytime  Workers in the vicinity of or involved in high-level noise to wear respective safety & protective gear i.e. earplugs & earmuffs  Appropriate selection of machinery  Proper storage, handling and disposal of new oil and used oil and related wastes  Maintain plant and equipment to avoid leaks  Maintenance of construction vehicles should be carried out in the contractors

Possible Impacts Water resource

Mitigation Measures

 Management  of  water  usage.  Avoid unnecessary  wastage  especially  at  the car washing bay

 Recycling of water during construction phase where possible

 Use of water conservation signs at the wash rooms and install water conserving taps

 Special attention should be paid to the sanitary facilities on site especially disposal of human waste.

Contractors lay down area

 Garbage  should  be  disposed  off in accordance with local Council requirements

 Enforce  speed  limits  for  construction vehicles  especially  along  road  linking to the site

Road safety

 Provide bill boards at the site/entrance to notify motorists about the development

 Ensure proper solid waste disposal and collection facilities

Public health and occupational safety

 Ensure effective wastewater management

 Design  of  sewerage  system  should  be as provided in the plans

 Provide First Aid kits on the site

 Sensitize stakeholders/workers on environmental management

 Workers should be trained on occupational  health  &  safety  and  first Aid administration

 Sensitise workers on HIV and AIDS

Mitigation Measures

Possible Impacts Vegetation

 Landscaping and planting all disturbed areas

 Planting  flowers  /  grassing  should  be done  just  before  the  rains  or  irrigated on dry spells.

 To enhance health and safety preparedness among stakeholders

Fire safety training/ Emergency response procedures (ERPs)

 Ensure  equipment  is  in  good  working condition.

 Put up emergency response contacts

 Put up ERP notification instructions

 Put  up  simple  instructions  on  how  to handle fires, armed robbery, floods

The full report of the proposed project is available for inspection during working hours at:

(a) The  Director-General,  National  Environment  Management Authority, Popo Road, off Mombasa Road, P.O. Box 6783900200, Nairobi.

(b) The  Permanent  Secretary,  Ministry  of  Environment  and Natural Resources, National Hospital Insurance Fund Building, Community, 4th Floor, P.O. Box 30521, Nairobi.

(c) Provincial Director of Environment, Nairobi Province.

(d) District Environment Officer, Nairobi West District.

B. M. LANGWEN, for Director-General, National Environment Management Authority.

THE KENYA CIVIL AVIATION AUTHORITY

APPLICATIONS FOR VARIATION OR ISSUE OF AIR SERVICE LICENCES

PURSUANT to the provisions of the Civil Aviation (Amendment) Act, 2002, notice is given that the applicants whose particulars are specified in the first column of the schedule below have applied for various air service licences.  The particulars of the applications are specified in the second column and the duration required for the licence is in the third column. Any objection or representation to any of the applications should be made in writing  to  the  Director  General,  Kenya  Civil  Aviation  Authority,  P.  O.  Box  30163  -  00100,  Fax:  254-20-822300,  Nairobi,  so  as  to  reach  the Authority within twenty-eight (28) days from the date of publication of this notice.

Every  objection  or  representation  should  be  sent  by  the  person  making  it  to  the  applicant  by  registered  mail  at  the  same  time  it  is  sent  to  the Authority.

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13792</span>
THE CO-OPERATIVE SOCIETIES ACT ( Cap . 490)

LIQUIDATION ORDER

WHEREAS  Munyaka  Farmers  Co-operative  Society  Limited, CS/2259  has  failed  to  file  returns  with  the  Commissioner  for  Cooperative Development for a period of three (3) years.

And pursuant to section 62 (1) (b), I am of the opinion that the said society should be dissolved.

Now therefore,  I  cancel  the  registration  of  the  society  and  order that it be liquidated.

And further, pursuant to section 65 of the said Act, I appoint P.A. K'Oremo, Co-operative Officer I, Headquarters, to be liquidator for a period  not  exceeding  one  year  and  authorize  him  to  take  into  his custody all the properties of the said society including such books and documents as are deemed necessary for completion of the liquidation.

Dated the 8th December, 2009.

F. F. ODHIAMBO,

Commissioner for Co-operative Development.

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13793</span>
THE CO-OPERATIVE SOCIETIES ACT ( Cap . 490)

CANCELLATION OF REGISTRATION

PURSUANT to section 62(C) of the  Co-operative Societies Act, the Commissioner for Co-operative Development cancels the registration  of  Kenya  National  Federation  of  Co-operatives  CS  No. 1068.

And in exercise of the powers conferred by Section 65 of the Cooperative Socities Act appoints Mr. Luke Omwansa, Senior Assisant Co-operative Officer, Nairobi and Roselyne Ragama , Legal Officer, Nairobi , to be  the liquidators for a period not exceeding one year and authorize  them  to  take  into  his  custody  all  the  property  of  the  said society including such books and documents as are deemed necessary for completion of the liquidation.

Dated the 16th December, 2009.

F. F. ODHIAMBO, Commissioner for Co-operative Development.

MERCY AWORI,

for Director-General.

<span style="background-color:#fff3cd;color:#1a1a1a;padding:0.15em 0.35em;border-radius:3px;font-weight:600;">GAZETTE NOTICE NO. 13794</span>
THE INSURANCE ACT

( Cap. 487)

PROPOSED TRANSFER OF THE LONG TERM INSURANCE BUSINESS OF BLUE SHIELD INSURANCE COMPANY LIMITED TO SHIELD ASSURANCE LIMITED

NOTICE OF APPLICATION-LONG TERM INSURANCE BUSINESS

NOTICE  is  given  of  the  proposed  transfer  of  the  long  term insurance  business  of  Blue  Shield  Insurance  Company  Limited  to Shield Assurance Company Limited. Both the transferor company and the transferee company are wholly owned subsidiary's of Blue Shield Holdings Limited.

The proposed transferor is Blue Shield Insurance  Company Limited  of  Blue  Shield  Towers,  Upper  Hill,  Mara  Road,  P.O.  Box 49610-00100, Nairobi ('BSIL').

The proposed transferee is Shield Assurance Company Limited of Blue Shield Towers, Upper Hill, Mara Road, P.O. Box 49610-00100, Nairobi ('SACL').

Prior to the transfer and subject to the approval of the Minister of Finance through the Commissioner of Insurance, BSIL will transfer its long term insurance business to SACL. BSIL will retain all its general insurance business. Details regarding the long term insurance business which  will  be  transferred  to  SACL  are  set  out  in  a  Statement  of Particulars which shall be available for public inspection as explained below.

Application  has  been  made  to  the  Commissioner  of  Insurance pursuant to the provisions of section 113 of the Insurance Act for his approval to the proposed acquisition.

Copies of a statement setting out particulars of the acquision have been deposited at the following offices:

Blue Shield Insurance Company Limited of Blue Shield Towers, Upper Hill, Mara Road, P.O. Box 49610-00100, Nairobi, contact person, Patrick Wanjala.

Shield Assurance Company Limited of Blue Shield Towers, Upper Hill, Mara Road, P.O. Box 49610-00100, Nairobi, contact person, Hillam Ngatia.

The Commissioner of insurance, 7th Floor, Zep Re Place, Upper Hill, Longonot Road, Nairobi, contact person, Agnes Ndirangu.

Any interested person (including any employee, director, shareholder or policyholder) who has reasonable grounds for believing that he would be adversely affected by the transfer, is invited to write or  make  oral  representations  to  the  Minister  within  thirty  (30)  days from  the  date  of  publication  of  this  notice,  statinig  the  grounds  on which he believes he would be adversely affected by the carrying out of the scheme of transfer.

Dated the 10th December, 2009.
